## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="54037-1682">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54037-1682">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="54037-1683">**ContentSet** 類別是分散式檔案系統 (DFS) Replication service 支援的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="54037-1683">The **ms-DFSR-ContentSet** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
